msg:! ! ! I don‚Äôt recommend this hotel very much. It doesn‚Äôt meet the five-star standards at all.

I chose this hotel to go to the safari park on the weekend. This hotel is close to Ueno and Shangdi and can arrange shuttle bus transfers. I checked Ctrip's 4.7 rating (high score). Based on the above advantages, I chose this Zhiwei hotel. Century Hotel.

But the actual experience is very different.

1. This hotel is a private enterprise and does not have much experience in five-star hotel management. The hotel service staff are mainly technical secondary school interns with good attitudes but no service experience.

2. The carpet in the hotel lobby is extremely unclean, even very dirty

3. The sound insulation is extremely poor, the walls are very thin, and you can clearly hear the voices next door. I went to bed at 10 o'clock that night and was woken up by the sound of the TV next door at 1:30 in the morning. If you want to have a peaceful sleep, don't choose this place. Hotel. The windows of the room were single-layer glass, and at around six o'clock in the morning, I was woken up again by the sound of firecrackers far outside the window. The room door has no soundproofing effect, and the sound from the corridor can be heard clearly.

4. The room facilities are very low, the TV screen is very small, the hair dryer has no quality at all (the wind power is very small), the toilet has to walk for a minute from the bed, the room feels large and empty, and the hotel is not willing to spend on hardware facilities Input costs.

5. The breakfast in the restaurant has a single variety. The only fruits available that day are watermelon and oranges.

6. The commercial street inside the hotel is messy, and all the shops in the commercial street are outsourced. There is a supermarket (actually a small shop) in the hotel. The price is slightly expensive, but the hygienic environment is worrying. There are massage parlors, bakeries, and souvenir shops in the commercial street. , game rooms, and nursing home sales departments gathered together, and it was unclear whether the hotel's strategic positioning was a parent-child hotel or a resort hotel.
